width: 100%" class="gcui-scientology-org-intro-image gcui-scientology-org-image" src="http://maps.google.com/maps/api/staticmap?center=29.4708,-98.4951&amp;zoom=14&amp;size=250x182&amp;maptype=roadmap&amp;markers=color:blue|29.4708,-98.4951&amp;sensor=false"></a>                  <div style="padding-bottom: 15px;"><a class="title-light" href="/directions.html">MAP &amp; DIRECTIONS</a></div>              </div>             <div class="col col-xs-12 col-sm-6">                  <div class="org-intro-data" id="org-intro-data-1">                     <p><strong>Location:</strong></p>                     <p>                         244 W. Olmos Drive<br>                         San Antonio,  TX 78212<br>                         <span class="nowidows">                             United States                         </span>                     </p>                     <p><a href="/directions.html">                         Map and Directions »                     </a></p>                 </div>                                       <div class="org-intro-data" id="org-intro-data-3">                         <p>                                                                                           » Phone: <a href="tel:+12108182868">210-818-2868</a><br>                                                                                   </p>                     </div>                                                 </div>         </div>      </div> </div>  <div class="article blocked-hover col-xs-12">     <div class="pb3 pt2">          <h3>             <a class="title-light" href="/what-is-scientology.html?link=bodytitle" target="_self">WHAT IS SCIENTOLOGY? </a>         </h3>          <p>Scientology is a religion in its highest meaning, as it helps bring Man to total freedom and truth. The essential tenets of Scientology are these: </p>          <div class="pl2"><p>You are an immortal spiritual being.</p> <p>Your experience extends well beyond a single lifetime. And your capabilities are unlimited, even if not presently realized.</p> <p>Furthermore, Man is basically good. He is seeking to survive. And his survival depends upon himself and his fellows and his attainment of brotherhood with the universe.</p> </div>          <p>             <a class="learn-more right" href="/what-is-scientology.html?link=body-learnmore">learn more </a>         </p>         <div class="clearfix"></div>      </div> </div>  <div class="article blocked-hover">      <div class="pb3 pt2 meet-a-scn">          <h3>             <a class="title-light" href="/meet-a-scientologist.html?videoid=meetscn_jackf&amp;region=northamerica" target="_self">MEET A SCIENTOLOGIST </a>         </h3>          <div class="row pt1">             <div class="col col-xs-12 col-sm-7 pr3">      <p>Who are Scientologists? Meet Jack, an owner of a classic car restoration business.</p> <p>“I've been a Scientologist since 1976,” says Jack. “Just the miracle of being able to have a very wonderful family, stable life and be able to achieve my goals. I dreamed this thing up and it's been successful and each and everything that I've done has been successful because I applied what I learned in Scientology.”</p>              </div>             <div class="col col-xs-12 col-sm-5 inline-meet-a-scn">                  <span style="position: relative; cursor: pointer;" onclick="location='/meet-a-scientologist.html?videoid=meetscn_jackf&amp;region=northamerica'; return false;">                     <img src="/f.edgesuite.net/imagecache/scalefit-400x600@as=1@qa=85/data/shared/web/assets/videos/master_thumbs/meetscn_jackf.jpg">                     <div class="center-playbutton-overlay video-slide-overlay" style="display: block !important;"></div>                 </span>                  <div style="padding-top: 7px;
